This taint effect:\n- **Prevents new pods from being scheduled** (like `NoSchedule`)\n- **Removes the node from Service EndpointSlices** (affecting traffic routing)\n- **Does NOT evict existing pods** (unlike `NoExecute`)\n\n## Files Created/Modified\n\n### 1. This new taint effect prevents pod scheduling and removes nodes from service traffic, without evicting existing pods.\n\n## What is NoScheduleNoTraffic?\n\nA new taint effect that combines characteristics of multiple existing effects:\n\n- **Prevents Scheduling** (like `NoSchedule`): New pods cannot be scheduled on the node unless they tolerate the taint\n- **Removes from Traffic** (unique): The node is excluded from service EndpointSlices, preventing traffic routing\n- **No Eviction** (unlike `NoExecute`): Existing pods are NOT evicted when the taint is applied\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Applying the Taint\n```bash\nkubectl taint nodes my-node maintenance=true:NoScheduleNoTraffic\n```\n\n### Creating a Tolerating Pod\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Pod\nmetadata:\n  name: maintenance-pod\nspec:\n  tolerations:\n  - key: maintenance\n    operator: Equal\n    value: \"true\"\n    effect: NoScheduleNoTraffic\n  containers:\n  - name: app\n    image: myapp:latest\n```\n\n## Implementation Contents\n\n### Core Files (8 Go files + 3 documentation files)\n\n1. **Constant Definitions**\n   - `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types_taint_effect.go` - v1 This new taint effect prevents pod scheduling and removes nodes from service traffic, without evicting existing pods.\n\n## What is NoScheduleNoTraffic?\n\nA new taint effect that combines characteristics of multiple existing effects:\n\n- **Prevents Scheduling** (like `NoSchedule`): New pods cannot be scheduled on the node unless they tolerate the taint\n- **Removes from Traffic** (unique): The node is excluded from service EndpointSlices, preventing traffic routing\n- **No Eviction** (unlike `NoExecute`): Existing pods are NOT evicted when the taint is applied\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Applying the Taint\n```bash\nkubectl taint nodes my-node maintenance=true:NoScheduleNoTraffic\n```\n\n### Creating a Tolerating Pod\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Pod\nmetadata:\n  name: maintenance-pod\nspec:\n  tolerations:\n  - key: maintenance\n    operator: Equal\n    value: \"true\"\n    effect: NoScheduleNoTraffic\n  containers:\n  - name: app\n    image: myapp:latest\n```\n\n## Implementation Contents\n\n### Core Files (8 Go files + 3 documentation files)\n\n1. **Constant Definitions**\n   - `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types_taint_effect.go` - v1
